<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;5.02 </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On March&#160;12, 2020, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> US, Inc., a Delaware corporation <span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#8220;T-Mobile&#8221;),</span> announced that David Carey, Executive Vice President, Corporate Services of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will retire from his position effective April&#160;30, 2020. As previously disclosed, on February&#160;12, 2020, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> adopted the first amendment (the &#8220;Amendment&#8221;) to the compensation term sheet, dated as of April&#160;28,&#160;2018, with Mr.&#160;Carey.&#160;A copy of the Amendment will subsequently be filed with the SEC. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;7.01 </td>

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">No Offer or Solicitation </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">This communication shall not constitute an offer to sell or the solicitation of an offer to buy any securities, nor shall there be any sale of securities in any jurisdiction in which such offer, solicitation or sale would be unlawful prior to registration or qualification under the securities laws of any such jurisdiction. No offering of securities shall be made except by means of a prospectus meeting the requirements of Section&#160;10 of the U.S. Securities Act of 1933, as amended. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Cautionary Statement Regarding Forward-Looking Statements </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">This communication contains certain forward-looking statements concerning <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> Sprint and the proposed transaction between <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and Sprint. All statements other than statements of fact, including information concerning future results, are forward-looking statements. These forward-looking statements are generally identified by the words &#8220;anticipate,&#8221; &#8220;believe,&#8221; &#8220;estimate,&#8221; &#8220;expect,&#8221; &#8220;intend,&#8221; &#8220;may,&#8221; &#8220;could&#8221; or similar expressions. There are several factors which could cause actual plans and results to differ materially from those expressed or implied in forward-looking statements. Such factors include, but are not limited to, the failure to obtain, or delays in obtaining, required regulatory approvals, and the risk that such approvals may result in the imposition of conditions that could adversely affect the combined company or the expected benefits of the proposed transaction, or the failure to satisfy any of the other conditions to the proposed transaction on a timely basis or at all; the occurrence of events that may give rise to a right of one or both of the parties to terminate the Business Combination Agreement; adverse effects on the market price of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> or Sprint&#8217;s common stock and on <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> or Sprint&#8217;s operating results because of a failure to complete the proposed transaction in the anticipated timeframe or at all;  <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>NEW T-MOBILE SLT ANNOUNCEMENT </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>To</B>: All Employees
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>From</B>: John Legere and Mike Sievert </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Subject:</B><B></B>&nbsp;A Message from John Legere and Mike Sievert&#151;Announcing New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> SLT! </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Team,</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We&#146;ve spent the last two years working to close our
transaction with Sprint to create the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> Along the way, many of you have been working to keep our business strong and to get integration plans underway so we can hit the ground running once this
deal finally closes. Every day, we get one step closer to making New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> a reality and we can&#146;t wait to get started changing the game &#150; AGAIN! We are so excited to see this team supercharge our <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> strategy, build a 5G network unlike anything the world has ever seen, and create jobs and career growth opportunities for so many of our employees. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">So, if we sound a little fired up about our future together&#133; it&#146;s because we are! </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">To create this future, we need to bring together the BEST of BOTH <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint &#150; the best of our people
and cultures.&nbsp;We also need to think differently about how we operate as a much larger company, without leaving behind the fast-paced entrepreneurial style that got us here. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As a company with the revenue profile of a Fortune 40 (by the way, wow!) &#150; we will need to ensure our business is focused on long term value
creation.&nbsp;We have a winning strategy today that has delivered incredible results over the last 7 years, but as we think about the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> we have to ensure our organization is set up to operate with
distinct lines of businesses and functions in order to help us achieve scale.&nbsp;This will require our leaders to invest even more time and energy on strategy and forward-looking topics to grow and compete in new ways.&nbsp;The New <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will need to deliver on even bigger cross-functional initiatives while pursuing businesses outside of core smartphone offerings. We will need to be a company with a growth mindset, but still have a
cost-conscious culture, and while all of this will be a difficult balance, we are confident that we have chosen the right leadership team to get it done. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">To build the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> we have chosen a team of amazing executives &#150; a solid, integrated team with deep
industry experience, an unwavering passion for customers and the willingness to battle and win in wireless and beyond! Together, we will need to build a culture that supports our respective missions&#151;taking the good from both <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">It is with that mindset that today, we are naming the executives who will serve as members of
the<U>&nbsp;New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Senior Leadership Team</U> (SLT), after the transaction closes and our companies come together. This team will lead the way as we build this future together! These changes will be
effective as of the closing of the transaction, also known as &#147;Day Zero&#148; of The New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>NEW T-MOBILE SLT ANNOUNCEMENT </B></P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><B>First</B></U>, let&#146;s discuss <U><B>Finance</B></U> and
<U><B>Technology</B></U>, who focus on our business from left to right.&nbsp;We&#146;re starting here because quite simply, New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> aspirations are centered on our ability to deliver on our
financials and to build the world&#146;s best 5G Network: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Finance</U>: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><B>Braxton Carter</B></U> will continue to serve as our Executive Vice President and Chief Financial Officer as a CEO direct report. Braxton joined MetroPCS
in 2001, where he also held the CFO role, and joined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> in 2013, upon closing the MetroPCS merger. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> team knows Braxton as the Magenta Cowboy&#151;a
financial wizard who has helped us build a company that has translated our customer growth over the last 7 years into strong financial performance. Braxton&#146;s leadership will be instrumental in our effort to continue <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> record of financial discipline and success as New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><B>Susan Loosmore</B></U> will serve as our new Executive Vice President, Financial Planning&nbsp;&amp; Analysis, reporting to Braxton. Susan has more than
23 years of wireless industry experience and has been with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> for over a decade, having served in several finance-related positions, including her most recent role as Senior Vice President of Financial
Planning&nbsp;&amp; Analysis. Susan knows the nuts and bolts of the business better than anyone and has helped <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> exceed our financial and operational goals at every step. Please join us in

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><B>Neville Ray</B></U> will continue to serve as our President of Technology, as a CEO direct report. Neville joined
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> 20 years ago, in April 2000, and has been plotting the future of our network ever since! He is the man responsible for building our 4G LTE network from the ground up, going from ZERO POPs of LTE at
the beginning of 2013 to 327&nbsp;million today. Neville and team also delivered America&#146;s first, largest and only nationwide 5G network. Neville is a respected industry icon (Thankfully, he&#146;s OUR industry icon!). He and his team will lead
our network and technology agenda into the 5G era! </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Abdul Saad</U></B> will serve as our Executive Vice President and Chief Technology Officer,
reporting into Neville. Abdul joined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> over 19 years ago and has been the strategic mastermind behind the innovation and growth of our network. Abdul&#146;s expanded role as a member of SLT is
well-timed as we prepare to embark on our future as the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and continue to lead the industry with nationwide 5G. Please join us in congratulating Abdul on his recent promotion! </P>

failure to obtain, or delays in obtaining, required regulatory approvals, and the risk that such approvals may result in the imposition of conditions that could adversely affect the combined company or the expected benefits of the proposed
transaction, or the failure to satisfy any of the other conditions to the proposed transaction on a timely basis or at all; the occurrence of events that may give rise to a right of one or both of the parties to terminate the Business Combination
Agreement; adverse effects on the market price of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or Sprint&#146;s common stock and on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or Sprint&#146;s operating results because of a
failure to complete the proposed transaction in the anticipated timeframe or at all; inability to obtain the financing contemplated to be obtained in connection with the proposed transaction on the expected terms or timing or at all; the ability of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Sprint and the combined company to make payments on debt or to repay existing or future indebtedness when due or to comply with the covenants contained therein; adverse changes in the ratings of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or Sprint&#146;s debt securities or adverse conditions in the credit markets; negative effects of the announcement, pendency or consummation of the transaction on the market price of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or Sprint&#146;s common stock and on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or Sprint&#146;s operating results, including as a result of changes in key customer, supplier, employee
or other business relationships; significant transaction costs, including financing costs, and unknown liabilities; failure to realize the expected benefits and synergies of the proposed transaction in the expected timeframes or at all; costs or
difficulties related to the integration of Sprint&#146;s network and operations into <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile;</FONT> the risk of litigation or regulatory actions, including the antitrust litigation brought by the attorneys general
of certain states and the District of Columbia; the inability of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Sprint or the combined company to retain and hire key personnel; the risk that certain contractual restrictions contained in the
Business Combination Agreement during the pendency of the proposed transaction could adversely affect <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or Sprint&#146;s ability to pursue business opportunities or strategic transactions;
effects of changes in the regulatory environment in which <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint operate; changes in global, political, economic, business, competitive and market conditions; changes in tax and other laws and
regulations; and other risks and uncertainties detailed in the Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-4,</FONT> as well as in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT>
for the fiscal year ended December&nbsp;31, 2019 and in its subsequent reports on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Q,</FONT> including in the sections thereof captioned &#147;Risk Factors&#148; and &#147;Cautionary Statement Regarding
Forward-Looking Statements,&#148; as well as in its subsequent reports on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</FONT> all of which are filed with the SEC and available at www. sec. gov and www. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">t-mobile.</FONT>
com. Forward-looking statements are based on current expectations and assumptions, which are subject to risks and uncertainties that may cause actual results to differ materially from those expressed in or implied by such forward-looking statements.
Given these risks and uncertainties, persons reading this communication are cautioned not to place undue reliance on such forward-looking statements. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> assumes no obligation to update or revise the
information contained in this communication (whether as a result of new information, future events or otherwise), except as required by applicable law. </P>
